MylottoWorkspace<?php
// this is the mylottoexpert entire code live 
defined('_JEXEC') or die;

// --------------------------------------------------
// Bootstrap: Get common Joomla objects (no "use" in Sorcerer)
// --------------------------------------------------
$app  = \Joomla\CMS\Factory::getApplication();
$user = \Joomla\CMS\Factory::getUser();
$db   = \Joomla\CMS\Factory::getDbo();
// FIND-AND-REPLACE: Added UTF-8 charset declaration per requirements
\Joomla\CMS\Factory::getDocument()->setCharset('utf-8');

if ($user->guest) {
    $app->enqueueMessage('You must be logged in to view or save your predictions.', 'error');
    $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::base() . 'index.php?option=com_users&view=login');
    exit;
}
// --------------------------------------------------
// Helper Functions (must be in the first PHP block for Sorcerer)
// --------------------------------------------------
/**
 * User profile prefs (stored in #__user_profiles)
 */
function mylottoexpertGetUserPref($db, $userId, $key, $default = '1') {
    $query = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->select($db->quoteName('profile_value'))
        ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_profiles'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . (int)$userId)
        ->where($db->quoteName('profile_key') . ' = ' . $db->quote('mylotto.' . $key))
        ->order($db->quoteName('ordering') . ' ASC')
        ->setLimit(1);
    $db->setQuery($query);
    $val = $db->loadResult();
    if ($val === null || $val === '') return $default;
    $decoded = json_decode($val, true);
    if (json_last_error() === JSON_ERROR_NONE) {
        return (string)($decoded ?? $default);
    }
    return (string)$val;
}

function mylottoexpertSetUserPref($db, $userId, $key, $value) {
    $value = (string)$value;
    $query = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->select('COUNT(*)')
        ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_profiles'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . (int)$userId)
        ->where($db->quoteName('profile_key') . ' = ' . $db->quote('mylotto.' . $key));
    $db->setQuery($query);
    $exists = (int)$db->loadResult() > 0;

    if ($exists) {
        $query = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->update($db->quoteName('#__user_profiles'))
            ->set($db->quoteName('profile_value') . ' = ' . $db->quote(json_encode($value)))
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . (int)$userId)
            ->where($db->quoteName('profile_key') . ' = ' . $db->quote('mylotto.' . $key));
    } else {
        $columns = ['user_id','profile_key','profile_value','ordering'];
        $values  = [
            (int)$userId,
            $db->quote('mylotto.' . $key),
            $db->quote(json_encode($value)),
            0
        ];
        $query = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->insert($db->quoteName('#__user_profiles'))
            ->columns(array_map([$db,'quoteName'], $columns))
            ->values(implode(',', $values));
    }
    $db->setQuery($query);
    $db->execute();
}

/**
 * Format a percentage for labels without unnecessary trailing zeros.
 */
function mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($value)
{
    if ($value === null || $value === '') {
        return '';
    }

    $value = round((float)$value, 1);

    if (abs($value - round($value)) < 0.05) {
        return (string)((int)round($value));
    }

    return rtrim(rtrim(number_format($value, 1, '.', ''), '0'), '.');
}

function mylottoexpertNormalizeBlendKey($value)
{
    $value = strtolower(trim((string)$value));
    $value = preg_replace('/[^a-z0-9]+/', ' ', $value);
    return trim(preg_replace('/\s+/', ' ', $value));
}

function mylottoexpertClampBlendPercent($value)
{
    if ($value === null || $value === '') {
        return null;
    }

    $value = (float)$value;
    if ($value < 0) {
        $value = 0.0;
    }
    if ($value > 100) {
        $value = 100.0;
    }

    return $value;
}

function mylottoexpertResolveBlendStrategyLabel($strategyKey, $ai)
{
    $canonicalMap = array(
        'skip pattern boost' => 'Skip Pattern Boost',
        'skip pattern'       => 'Skip Pattern Boost',
        'skip forward'       => 'Skip Pattern Boost',
        'skip heavy'         => 'Skip Pattern Boost',
        'skip boost'         => 'Skip Pattern Boost',
        'balanced mix'       => 'Balanced Mix',
        'balanced'           => 'Balanced Mix',
        'ai forward'         => 'AI-Forward',
        'ai heavy'           => 'AI-Forward',
        'ai forward blend'   => 'AI-Forward'
    );

    if ($strategyKey !== '' && isset($canonicalMap[$strategyKey])) {
        return $canonicalMap[$strategyKey];
    }

    if ($ai !== null) {
        if ($ai >= 65) {
            return 'AI-Forward';
        }
        if ($ai <= 40) {
            return 'Skip Pattern Boost';
        }
        return 'Balanced Mix';
    }

    return '';
}

function mylottoexpertResolveBlendExplanation($strategyLabel)
{
    if ($strategyLabel === 'AI-Forward') {
        return 'More AI-driven weighting';
    }
    if ($strategyLabel === 'Balanced Mix') {
        return 'Balanced SKAI mix';
    }
    if ($strategyLabel === 'Skip Pattern Boost') {
        return 'More skip-pattern emphasis';
    }
    return '';
}

function mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($row, $settings)
{
    $skip = null;
    $ai   = null;

    if (is_array($settings)) {
        $settingsPairs = array(
            array('skai_blend_skip_pct', 'skai_blend_ai_pct'),
            array('blend_skip_pct', 'blend_ai_pct'),
            array('skip_pct', 'ai_pct')
        );

        foreach ($settingsPairs as $pair) {
            if ($skip === null && array_key_exists($pair[0], $settings) && $settings[$pair[0]] !== '' && $settings[$pair[0]] !== null) {
                $skip = mylottoexpertClampBlendPercent($settings[$pair[0]]);
            }
            if ($ai === null && array_key_exists($pair[1], $settings) && $settings[$pair[1]] !== '' && $settings[$pair[1]] !== null) {
                $ai = mylottoexpertClampBlendPercent($settings[$pair[1]]);
            }
        }
    }

    if ($skip === null) {
        foreach (array('skai_blend_skip_pct', 'blend_skip_pct', 'skip_pct') as $rowKey) {
            $rowSkip = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, $rowKey);
            if ($rowSkip !== null && $rowSkip !== '') {
                $skip = mylottoexpertClampBlendPercent($rowSkip);
                break;
            }
        }
    }
    if ($ai === null) {
        foreach (array('skai_blend_ai_pct', 'blend_ai_pct', 'ai_pct') as $rowKey) {
            $rowAi = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, $rowKey);
            if ($rowAi !== null && $rowAi !== '') {
                $ai = mylottoexpertClampBlendPercent($rowAi);
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    $strategyKey = '';
    if (is_array($settings)) {
        if (!empty($settings['strategy'])) {
            $strategyKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeBlendKey($settings['strategy']);
        } elseif (!empty($settings['blend'])) {
            $strategyKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeBlendKey($settings['blend']);
        }
    }

    if ($strategyKey === '') {
        $rowStrategy = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'strategy');
        $rowBlend = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'blend');
        if ($rowStrategy !== null && $rowStrategy !== '') {
            $strategyKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeBlendKey($rowStrategy);
        } elseif ($rowBlend !== null && $rowBlend !== '') {
            $strategyKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeBlendKey($rowBlend);
        }
    }

    if ($skip === null && $ai === null && $strategyKey !== '') {
        $presetMap = array(
            'skip pattern boost' => array(75.0, 25.0),
            'skip pattern'       => array(75.0, 25.0),
            'skip forward'       => array(75.0, 25.0),
            'skip heavy'         => array(75.0, 25.0),
            'skip boost'         => array(75.0, 25.0),
            'balanced mix'       => array(45.0, 55.0),
            'balanced'           => array(45.0, 55.0),
            'ai forward'         => array(25.0, 75.0),
            'ai heavy'           => array(25.0, 75.0),
            'ai forward blend'   => array(25.0, 75.0)
        );
        if (isset($presetMap[$strategyKey])) {
            $skip = $presetMap[$strategyKey][0];
            $ai   = $presetMap[$strategyKey][1];
        }
    }

    if ($skip === null && $ai !== null) {
        $derivedSkip = 100.0 - (float)$ai;
        if ($derivedSkip >= 0 && $derivedSkip <= 100) {
            $skip = $derivedSkip;
        }
    }
    if ($ai === null && $skip !== null) {
        $derivedAi = 100.0 - (float)$skip;
        if ($derivedAi >= 0 && $derivedAi <= 100) {
            $ai = $derivedAi;
        }
    }

    $strategyLabel = mylottoexpertResolveBlendStrategyLabel($strategyKey, $ai);
    $aiText = mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($ai);
    $skipText = mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($skip);
    $primary = '';
    if ($aiText !== '' && $strategyLabel !== '') {
        $primary = $aiText . '% AI - ' . $strategyLabel;
    } elseif ($aiText !== '') {
        $primary = $aiText . '% AI';
    } elseif ($skipText !== '') {
        $primary = $skipText . '% Skip';
    }

    $technical = '';
    if ($skip !== null && $ai !== null) {
        $technical = 'Skip ' . mylottoexpertFormatPrecisePercent($skip) . '% | AI ' . mylottoexpertFormatPrecisePercent($ai) . '%';
    } elseif ($ai !== null) {
        $technical = 'AI ' . mylottoexpertFormatPrecisePercent($ai) . '%';
    } elseif ($skip !== null) {
        $technical = 'Skip ' . mylottoexpertFormatPrecisePercent($skip) . '%';
    }

    return array(
        'skip' => $skip,
        'ai' => $ai,
        'strategy_key' => $strategyKey,
        'strategy_label' => $strategyLabel,
        'explanation' => mylottoexpertResolveBlendExplanation($strategyLabel),
        'primary' => $primary,
        'technical' => $technical
    );
}

function mylottoexpertResolveBlendPair($row, $settings)
{
    $blendInfo = mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($row, $settings);
    return array($blendInfo['skip'], $blendInfo['ai']);
}

/**
 * Build a human-readable SKAI blend label from the resolved settings source of truth.
 */
function mylottoexpertBuildSkaiBlendLabel($row)
{
    $settings = mylottoexpertResolveEffectiveSettings($row);
    $blendInfo = mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($row, $settings);
    return (string)$blendInfo['primary'];
}

function mylottoexpertNormalizeLotteryKey($value)
{
    $value = (string)$value;
    $value = strtolower(trim($value));
    $value = preg_replace('/[^a-z0-9]+/', ' ', $value);
    $value = trim(preg_replace('/\s+/', ' ', $value));
    return $value;
}

function mylottoexpertIsEuroMillionsLottery($stateName, $gameName)
{
    $stateKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeLotteryKey($stateName);
    $gameKey  = mylottoexpertNormalizeLotteryKey($gameName);
    $comboKey = trim($stateKey . ' ' . $gameKey);

    return ($gameKey === 'euromillions'
        || $gameKey === 'euro millions'
        || $comboKey === 'euromillions'
        || $comboKey === 'euro millions'
        || $stateKey === 'euromillions'
        || $stateKey === 'euro millions');
}

function mylottoexpertBuildEuroMillionsLogoPath($gameName)
{
    $gameName = (string)$gameName;
    $candidates = array(
        '/images/lottodb/us/uk/euromillions.png',
        '/images/lottodb/us/UK/euromillions.png'
    );

    foreach ($candidates as $rel) {
        if ($rel !== '' && is_file(JPATH_ROOT . $rel)) {
            return array(
                'path'   => $rel,
                'exists' => true,
                'alt'    => ($gameName !== '' ? $gameName : 'EuroMillions') . ' logo'
            );
        }
    }

    return array(
        'path'   => $candidates[0],
        'exists' => false,
        'alt'    => ($gameName !== '' ? $gameName : 'EuroMillions') . ' logo'
    );
}

function mylottoexpertIsValidSavedLabel($label)
{
    $label = trim((string)$label);
    if ($label === '') {
        return false;
    }

    return !in_array(strtolower($label), array('default', 'n/a', 'na', '-', '--', 'null'), true);
}

function mylottoexpertFormatPrecisePercent($value)
{
    if ($value === null || $value === '') {
        return '';
    }
    return number_format((float)$value, 2, '.', '');
}

function mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, $key)
{
    if (is_array($row)) {
        return array_key_exists($key, $row) ? $row[$key] : null;
    }
    if (is_object($row)) {
        return isset($row->$key) ? $row->$key : null;
    }
    return null;
}

function mylottoexpertResolveEffectiveSettings($row)
{
    $settings = array();
    $jsonCandidates = array('settings_json', 'settings', 'params_json', 'params', 'digit_probabilities');

    foreach ($jsonCandidates as $jsonKey) {
        $rawJson = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, $jsonKey);
        if ($rawJson === null || $rawJson === '') {
            continue;
        }
        $decoded = json_decode((string)$rawJson, true);
        if (json_last_error() === JSON_ERROR_NONE && is_array($decoded)) {
            $settings = $decoded;
            break;
        }
    }

    if (!is_array($settings)) {
        $settings = array();
    }

    $dbFallbackKeys = array(
        'label','skai_run_mode','pure_mode',
        'skai_blend_skip_pct','skai_blend_ai_pct',
        'blend_skip_pct','blend_ai_pct','skip_pct','ai_pct',
        'epochs','batch_size','dropout_rate','learning_rate',
        'activation_function','hidden_layers','recency_decay',
        'walks','burn_in','laplace_k','decay','chain_len',
        'draws_analyzed','freq_weight','skip_weight','hist_weight',
        'draws_used','skip_window','auto_tune','tune_used','best_window',
        'sampling_temperature','diversity_penalty','gap_scale',
        'skai_window_size','skai_top_n_numbers','skai_top_n_combos',
        'profile','training_style','risk_profile','strategy','blend','blend_percent'
    );

    foreach ($dbFallbackKeys as $key) {
        if (!array_key_exists($key, $settings) || $settings[$key] === '' || $settings[$key] === null) {
            $dbVal = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, $key);
            if ($dbVal !== null && $dbVal !== '') {
                $settings[$key] = $dbVal;
            }
        }
    }

    return $settings;
}

function mylottoexpertBuildPreciseBlendDisplay($row, $settings)
{
    $blendInfo = mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($row, $settings);
    return (string)$blendInfo['technical'];
}

function mylottoexpertResolveRunDisplayInfo($row, array $methodLabels)
{
    $settings = mylottoexpertResolveEffectiveSettings($row);
    $src = (string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'source') ?: '');

    $baseLabel = isset($methodLabels[$src])
        ? (string)$methodLabels[$src]
        : ucwords(str_replace('_', ' ', $src));

    $savedLabel = '';
    if (isset($settings['label']) && mylottoexpertIsValidSavedLabel($settings['label'])) {
        $savedLabel = trim((string)$settings['label']);
    } else {
        $rowLabel = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'label');
        if (mylottoexpertIsValidSavedLabel($rowLabel)) {
            $savedLabel = trim((string)$rowLabel);
        }
    }

    $runModeRaw = '';
    if (!empty($settings['skai_run_mode'])) {
        $runModeRaw = (string)$settings['skai_run_mode'];
    } else {
        $rowRunMode = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'skai_run_mode');
        if (!empty($rowRunMode)) {
            $runModeRaw = (string)$rowRunMode;
        }
    }

    $runMode = $runModeRaw !== '' ? ucwords(str_replace('_', ' ', $runModeRaw)) : '';
    $blendInfo = mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($row, $settings);
    $modeDisplay = $runMode;
    if ($blendInfo['primary'] !== '') {
        $modeDisplay = trim($modeDisplay !== '' ? ($modeDisplay . ' - ' . $blendInfo['primary']) : $blendInfo['primary']);
    }

    if ($src === 'skai_prediction' && $modeDisplay !== '') {
        $effectiveLabel = $modeDisplay;
    } else {
        $effectiveLabel = $savedLabel !== '' ? $savedLabel : ($runMode !== '' ? $runMode : $baseLabel);
    }

    return array(
        'base_label'        => $baseLabel,
        'label'             => $effectiveLabel,
        'saved_label'       => $savedLabel,
        'mode'              => $modeDisplay,
        'run_mode'          => $runMode,
        'blend_display'     => (string)$blendInfo['primary'],
        'blend_technical'   => (string)$blendInfo['technical'],
        'blend_strategy'    => (string)$blendInfo['strategy_label'],
        'blend_explainer'   => (string)$blendInfo['explanation'],
        'source'            => $src,
        'settings'          => $settings
    );
}

/**
 * Derive a concise label from a saved run row for the Best Settings Snapshot.
 * Shows method name and optional run mode / template name.
 */
function mylottoexpertBuildBestSettingsSummary(array $row, array $methodLabels)
{
    $disp = mylottoexpertResolveRunDisplayInfo($row, $methodLabels);
    $label = (string)$disp['base_label'];

    $templateName = '';
    if (isset($row['template_name']) && $row['template_name'] !== null && $row['template_name'] !== '') {
        $templateName = (string)$row['template_name'];
    } elseif (isset($row['settings_template_name']) && $row['settings_template_name'] !== null && $row['settings_template_name'] !== '') {
        $templateName = (string)$row['settings_template_name'];
    }
    if ($templateName !== '') {
        return $label . ' - ' . $templateName;
    }

    if ((string)$disp['source'] === 'skai_prediction') {
        $modeLabel = (string)$disp['mode'];
        if ($modeLabel === '') {
            $modeLabel = 'Default';
        }
        return $label . ' - ' . $modeLabel;
    }

    if ($disp['saved_label'] !== '' && $disp['saved_label'] !== $label) {
        return $disp['saved_label'];
    }

    return $label;
}

function mylottoexpertBuildActionTweakFromSettings(array $settings)
{
    $src = isset($settings['source']) ? (string)$settings['source'] : '';
    $action = 'Add more saved runs before making a setting change recommendation.';
    $stable = 'Keep the current setup stable until you have enough repeat evidence to isolate one variable.';

    if ($src === 'skai_prediction') {
        $bestWindowOn = (!empty($settings['best_window']) && (string)$settings['best_window'] !== '0');
        $windowSize   = isset($settings['skai_window_size']) ? (float)$settings['skai_window_size'] : 0.0;
        $autoTuneOn   = (!empty($settings['auto_tune']) && (string)$settings['auto_tune'] !== '0');
        $divPenalty   = isset($settings['diversity_penalty']) ? (float)$settings['diversity_penalty'] : 0.0;

        if (!$bestWindowOn) {
            $action = 'Turn on Best Window before changing anything else. That is the cleanest next test for this SKAI setup.';
            $stable = 'Keep the current run mode, blend, and window size unchanged while you test Best Window.';
        } elseif ($windowSize > 50) {
            $action = 'Reduce the SKAI window slightly to tighten the pool and see whether overlap improves.';
            $stable = 'Keep the current run mode and blend stable while you test a smaller window.';
        } elseif (!$autoTuneOn) {
            $action = 'Enable Auto-tune next so the setup can adapt without changing the current mode or blend.';
            $stable = 'Do not change the run mode, blend, or Best Window at the same time.';
        } elseif ($divPenalty > 0.65) {
            $action = 'Reduce diversity penalty one step to see whether the repeated-number cluster becomes tighter.';
            $stable = 'Hold the current run mode, blend, and window size steady during that test.';
        } else {
            $action = 'Increase or decrease diversity penalty one step at a time to refine clustering without breaking the current signal.';
            $stable = 'Keep the current run mode, blend, window size, and Best Window setting stable.';
        }
    } elseif ($src === 'skip_hit') {
        $skipWeight = isset($settings['skip_weight']) ? (float)$settings['skip_weight'] : 1.0;
        $histWeight = isset($settings['hist_weight']) ? (float)$settings['hist_weight'] : 1.0;
        if ($skipWeight > ($histWeight * 1.3)) {
            $action = 'Increase historical weight slightly so history has more influence against the current skip bias.';
            $stable = 'Keep draws analyzed stable while you test weighting.';
        } else {
            $action = 'Increase or decrease draws analyzed by about 20 while keeping the weight balance unchanged.';
            $stable = 'Hold skip weight and historical weight steady for the next test.';
        }
    } elseif ($src === 'mcmc_prediction') {
        $action = 'Increase or decrease chain length next while keeping the decay rate unchanged.';
        $stable = 'Keep recency decay stable so you can isolate the effect of chain length.';
    } elseif ($src === 'ai_prediction') {
        $action = 'Adjust recency decay slightly before you touch epochs or architecture.';
        $stable = 'Keep epochs, hidden layers, and dropout unchanged during that test.';
    }

    return array('action' => $action, 'stable' => $stable);
}

function mylottoexpertRenderModuleById($moduleId, $style = 'none') {
    $moduleId = (int) $moduleId;
    if ($moduleId <= 0) {
        return '';
    }

    $module = \Joomla\CMS\Helper\ModuleHelper::getModuleById($moduleId);

    if (empty($module) || empty($module->module)) {
        return '';
    }

    return \Joomla\CMS\Helper\ModuleHelper::renderModule($module, ['style' => (string) $style]);
}


// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// New Features toggle (persisted in #__user_profiles)
// Stored as '1' (show) / '0' (hide).
// We can safely call helpers before their textual definition (PHP parses file first).
$showNewFeatures = mylottoexpertGetUserPref($db, (int) $user->id, 'showNewFeatures', '1') === '1';

// Allow POST toggle via form
if ($app->input->getMethod() === 'POST' && $app->input->post->get('toggle_new_features', '', 'STRING') !== '') {
    if (!\Joomla\CMS\Session\Session::checkToken('post')) {
        die('Invalid Token');
    }
    $newVal = $app->input->post->get('new_features_enabled', '0', 'STRING') === '1' ? '1' : '0';
    mylottoexpertSetUserPref($db, (int) $user->id, 'showNewFeatures', $newVal);
    $showNewFeatures = ($newVal === '1');
}
// --------------------------------------------------
// Prediction List: Recency Sort Preference (persisted in #__user_profiles)
// --------------------------------------------------
$predSortPref = mylottoexpertGetUserPref($db, (int)$user->id, 'predSort', 'desc'); // 'desc' = newest→oldest (default)
$predSortDir  = (strtolower($predSortPref) === 'asc') ? 'ASC' : 'DESC';

// Allow POST change via form
if ($app->input->getMethod() === 'POST' && $app->input->post->get('change_sort_dir', '', 'STRING') !== '') {
    if (!\Joomla\CMS\Session\Session::checkToken('post')) {
        die('Invalid Token');
    }
    $dir = strtolower($app->input->post->get('pred_sort_dir', 'desc', 'STRING'));
    $dir = ($dir === 'asc') ? 'asc' : 'desc';
    mylottoexpertSetUserPref($db, (int)$user->id, 'predSort', $dir);
    $predSortDir = ($dir === 'asc') ? 'ASC' : 'DESC';
}

// --------------------------------------------------
// Handle Prediction Deletion / Template Actions
// IMPORTANT: Only enforce CSRF when THIS page's actions are triggered.
// This avoids breaking unrelated module POSTs that may target this URL.
// --------------------------------------------------

if ($app->input->getMethod() === 'POST') {

    // Detect whether this POST is intended for mylottoexpert actions
    $hasDashboardAction =
        ($app->input->post->getInt('delete_set', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->get('delete_set_selected', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->get('delete_all_predictions', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->get('delete_lottery_predictions', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('delete_setting_template', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->get('save_setting_template', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->get('toggle_new_features', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->get('change_sort_dir', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('save_strategy_set', 0) > 0);

    if ($hasDashboardAction && !\Joomla\CMS\Session\Session::checkToken('post')) {
        $app->enqueueMessage('Your session expired. Please refresh and try again.', 'error');
        $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        exit;
    }

    // Delete single prediction (hardened: use Joomla input filtering)
    $id = $app->input->post->getInt('delete_set', 0);
    if ($id > 0) {

        $q = $db->getQuery(true)

            ->delete($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
            ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' = ' . $id)
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . (int) $user->id);

        $db->setQuery($q);
        try {
            $db->execute();
            $app->enqueueMessage('Prediction deleted.', 'message');
            $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        } catch (Exception $e) {
            $app->enqueueMessage('Error deleting: ' . $e->getMessage(), 'error');
        }
    }
    // Delete multiple predictions via PRC table checkboxes (comma-separated IDs)
    $__rawSelected = $app->input->post->get('delete_set_selected', '', 'STRING');
    if ($__rawSelected !== '') {
        // intval() cast ensures all values are pure integers; safe to embed directly in SQL.
        $__selectedIds = array_values(array_filter(array_map('intval', explode(',', $__rawSelected))));
        if (!empty($__selectedIds)) {
            $q = $db->getQuery(true)
                ->delete($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
                ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' IN (' . implode(',', $__selectedIds) . ')')
                ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . (int) $user->id);
            $db->setQuery($q);
            try {
                $db->execute();
                $count = count($__selectedIds);
                $app->enqueueMessage($count . ' prediction' . ($count !== 1 ? 's' : '') . ' deleted.', 'message');
                $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
            } catch (Exception $e) {
                $app->enqueueMessage('Error deleting: ' . $e->getMessage(), 'error');
            }
        }
    }

    // Delete all predictions (hardened: use Joomla input filtering)
    $doDeleteAll = $app->input->post->get('delete_all_predictions', '', 'STRING') !== '';
    if ($doDeleteAll) {
        $q = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->delete($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . (int) $user->id);

        $db->setQuery($q);
        try {
            $db->execute();
            $app->enqueueMessage('All predictions deleted.', 'message');
            $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        } catch (Exception $e) {
            $app->enqueueMessage('Error deleting all: ' . $e->getMessage(), 'error');
        }
    }

// Delete all predictions for a single lottery + draw date (group delete)  -  hardened input
$doGroupDelete = $app->input->post->get('delete_lottery_predictions', '', 'STRING') !== '';
$lotteryId     = $app->input->post->getInt('lottery_id', 0);
$drawDateRaw   = $app->input->post->getString('draw_date', '');
if ($doGroupDelete && $lotteryId && $drawDateRaw !== '') {
    $drawDate  = date('Y-m-d', strtotime($drawDateRaw)); // normalize

    $q = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->delete($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))

        ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . (int) $user->id)
        ->where($db->quoteName('lottery_id') . ' = ' . $lotteryId)
        // compare only date portion of next_draw_date
        ->where('DATE(' . $db->quoteName('next_draw_date') . ') = ' . $db->quote($drawDate));

    $db->setQuery($q);
    try {
        $db->execute();
        $app->enqueueMessage('Deleted all predictions for this draw.', 'message');
        $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
    } catch (Exception $e) {
        $app->enqueueMessage('Error deleting group: ' . $e->getMessage(), 'error');
    }
}

// Delete saved setting template (hardened: use Joomla input filtering)
$id = $app->input->post->getInt('delete_setting_template', 0);
if ($id > 0) {

        // $id already sanitized above
        $q = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->delete($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_settings'))

            ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' = ' . $id)
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . (int) $user->id);

        $db->setQuery($q);
        try {
            $db->execute();
            $app->enqueueMessage('Saved setting deleted.', 'message');
            $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        } catch (Exception $e) {
            $app->enqueueMessage('Error deleting saved setting: ' . $e->getMessage(), 'error');
        }
    }

    // Save prediction settings as a named template (hardened: use Joomla input filtering)
    if ($app->input->post->get('save_setting_template', '', 'STRING') !== '') {
        $settingName = trim($app->input->post->getString('setting_name', ''));
        $source      = $app->input->post->getString('source', '');
        $lotteryId   = $app->input->post->getInt('lottery_id', 0);
        $params      = [];

        // Define expected params based on source
        $keys = match ($source) {
            'ai_prediction'   => [
                'epochs', 'batch_size', 'dropout_rate',
                'learning_rate', 'activation_function',
                'hidden_layers', 'recency_decay',
            ],
            'skai_prediction' => [
                // Core neural hyperparameters
                'epochs', 'batch_size', 'dropout_rate',
                'learning_rate', 'activation_function',
                'hidden_layers', 'recency_decay',
                // Windows
                'skai_window_size', 'skip_window', 'draws_used', 'tuned_window',
                // Behavior & sampling
                'sampling_temperature', 'diversity_penalty', 'gap_scale',
                // Mode / automation
                'skai_run_mode', 'auto_tune', 'tune_used', 'best_window',
                // Smart blend / strategy
                'profile', 'training_style', 'strategy', 'blend',
                'skai_blend_skip_pct', 'skai_blend_ai_pct',
                'blend_skip_pct', 'blend_ai_pct',
                'skip_pct', 'ai_pct',
                // Output size
                'skai_top_n_numbers', 'skai_top_n_combos',
            ],
            'mcmc_prediction' => ['walks', 'burn_in', 'laplace_k', 'decay', 'chain_len'],
            'skip_hit'        => ['draws_analyzed', 'freq_weight', 'skip_weight', 'hist_weight'],
            default           => []
        };

        foreach ($keys as $k) {
            $val = $app->input->post->get($k, null, 'STRING'); // keep as STRING to avoid behavior changes
            if ($val !== null && $val !== '') {
                $params[$k] = $val;
            }
        }

        if ($settingName && $source && $lotteryId && $params) {
            $q = $db->getQuery(true)
                ->insert($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_settings'))
                ->columns(['user_id', 'lottery_id', 'source', 'setting_name', 'params'])
                ->values(implode(',', [
                    (int) $user->id,
                    $lotteryId,
                    $db->quote($source),
                    $db->quote($settingName),
                    $db->quote(json_encode($params))
                ]));

            $db->setQuery($q);
            try {
                $db->execute();
                $app->enqueueMessage('Settings saved.', 'message');
            } catch (Exception $e) {
                $app->enqueueMessage('Failed to save: ' . $e->getMessage(), 'error');
            }
        }
    }

    // Module keys needed for save_strategy_set source whitelisting below.
    // Defined here so it is available before the main render block (line ~1736).
    if (!isset($modules)) {
        $modules = array(
            array('key' => 'skip_hit',        'label' => 'SKIP Model',      'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Analyzes historical draw patterns'),
            array('key' => 'ai_prediction',   'label' => 'Neural Network',  'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Deep learning model trained on draw history'),
            array('key' => 'mcmc_prediction', 'label' => 'MCMC',            'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Statistical sampling method'),
            array('key' => 'heatmap',         'label' => 'Frequency Map',   'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Visual frequency analysis'),
            array('key' => 'skai_prediction', 'label' => 'SKAI Model',      'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Combines multiple analytical methods'),
        );
    }

    // Save Strategy Set (from Overview PRE-DRAW workspace)
    if ($app->input->post->getInt('save_strategy_set', 0) > 0) {
        // Require authenticated user
        if ($user->guest) {
            $app->enqueueMessage('You must be logged in to save a strategy set.', 'error');
            $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
            exit;
        }

        $__stLid  = $app->input->post->getInt('strategy_lottery_id', 0);
        $__stDate = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_draw_date', ''));
        $__stMain = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_main_numbers', ''));
        $__stExt  = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_extra_numbers', ''));
        $__stLbl  = substr(trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_label', '')), 0, 80);
        $__stSrc  = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_active_sources', ''));

        // Validate lottery_id exists in lotteries table
        $__stLidCheck = 0;
        if ($__stLid > 0) {
            $__qLid = $db->getQuery(true)->select('lottery_id')
                ->from($db->quoteName('#__lotteries'))
                ->where($db->quoteName('lottery_id') . ' = ' . (int)$__stLid);
            $db->setQuery($__qLid, 0, 1);
            $__stLidCheck = (int)$db->loadResult();
        }

        // Whitelist active sources against known module keys
        $__validSrcKeys = array_column($modules, 'key');
        $__stSrcKeys    = array_values(array_filter(
            array_map('trim', explode(',', $__stSrc)),
            static function($k) use ($__validSrcKeys) { return in_array($k, $__validSrcKeys, true); }
        ));

        // Parse and validate numbers (positive integers only)
        $__stMainNums = array_values(array_filter(array_map('intval',
            array_filter(explode(',', $__stMain), 'strlen')),
            static function($n) { return $n > 0; }));
        $__stExtNums  = array_values(array_filter(array_map('intval',
            array_filter(explode(',', $__stExt), 'strlen')),
            static function($n) { return $n > 0; }));

        // Normalize date; reject if unparseable
        $__stTs       = $__stDate !== '' ? strtotime($__stDate) : false;
        $__stNormDate = $__stTs !== false ? date('Y-m-d', $__stTs) : '';

        if ($__stLidCheck > 0 && $__stNormDate !== '' && count($__stMainNums) > 0) {
            $__stLabel = $__stLbl !== '' ? $__stLbl
                : 'Strategy Set - ' . date('Y-m-d H:i');
            $q = $db->getQuery(true)
                ->insert($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
                ->columns(['user_id','lottery_id','next_draw_date','source',
                           'label','main_numbers','extra_ball_numbers','date_saved'])
                ->values(implode(',', [
                    (int) $user->id,
                    $__stLidCheck,
                    $db->quote($__stNormDate),
                    $db->quote('strategy_set'),
                    $db->quote($__stLabel),
                    $db->quote(implode(',', $__stMainNums)),
                    $db->quote(implode(',', $__stExtNums)),
                    $db->quote(date('Y-m-d H:i:s'))
                ]));
            $db->setQuery($q);
            try {
                $db->execute();
                $app->enqueueMessage('Strategy saved to Saved Numbers.', 'message');
            } catch (Exception $e) {
                $app->enqueueMessage('Error saving strategy: ' . $e->getMessage(), 'error');
            }
        } else {
            $app->enqueueMessage('Please add at least one number before saving.', 'warning');
        }
        $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
    }
}

// --------------------------------------------------
// Echo your Sorcerer module
// --------------------------------------------------
echo mylottoexpertRenderModuleById((int) $params->get('header_module_id', 126), (string) $params->get('header_module_style', 'none'));

When the same numbers appear across independent methods, that creates an <strong>agreement signal</strong>. When those same methods or settings also score well after completed draws, that signal becomes more trustworthy.

// --------------------------------------------------
// Configuration Labels for prediction sources
// --------------------------------------------------
$sourceLabels = [
    'ai_prediction'    => 'Neural Network',
    'skip_hit'         => 'SKIP Model',
    'frequency'        => 'Frequency Map',
    'mcmc_prediction'  => 'MCMC',
    'heatmap'          => 'Frequency Map',
    'skai_prediction'  => 'SKAI Model',
];
$__methodLabels = $sourceLabels;

// Map source keys → short codes for compact display
$iconMap = [
    'ai_prediction'   => 'NN',
    'skip_hit'        => 'PA',
    'frequency'       => 'FM',
    'mcmc_prediction' => 'PS',
    'heatmap'         => 'FM',
    'skai_prediction' => 'HM',
