if (ovKpiMethods) { ovKpiMethods.textContent = String(methodsUsed); }
if (ovKpiOverlap) { ovKpiOverlap.textContent = String(overlapScore); }
if (ovKpiConf)    { ovKpiConf.textContent    = levelLabel; }
if (ovKpiConfCard) {
  var ovConfValEl = ovKpiConfCard.querySelector('[data-skai-kpi-conf]');
  if (ovConfValEl) {
    ovConfValEl.className = ovConfValEl.className
      .replace(/\bskai-ov-kpi-value--(accent|success|caution)\b/g, '')
      .replace(/\s{2,}/g, ' ')
      .replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
    if (levelLabel === 'High' || levelLabel === 'Balanced') {
      ovConfValEl.className += ' skai-ov-kpi-value--success';
    } else if (levelLabel === 'Single-method') {
      ovConfValEl.className += ' skai-ov-kpi-value--caution';
    } else {
      ovConfValEl.className += ' skai-ov-kpi-value--accent';
    }
  }
}
      }
    }
  });
  
//  -  Settings panels: default COLLAPSED; persist per run  - 
// Use delegation so clicks work reliably on mobile and future DOM changes.
document.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
  var toggle = ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('.settings-toggle') : null;
  if (!toggle) return;

  var card  = toggle.closest('.prediction-card');
  if (!card) return;
  var panel = card.querySelector('.settings-panel');
  if (!panel) return;

  var id     = card.getAttribute('data-set-id') || '';
  var openKey = 'settingsOpen_' + id;

  // Current open/closed from DOM (default collapsed)
  var isOpen = panel.classList.contains('open');

  // Toggle
  isOpen = !isOpen;
  panel.classList.toggle('open', isOpen);
  panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden', isOpen ? 'false' : 'true');
  toggle.textContent = isOpen ? 'Hide Details' : 'Details';
  toggle.setAttribute('title', isOpen ? 'Hide details' : 'Show details');
  toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');

  try { localStorage.setItem(openKey, String(isOpen)); } catch(e){}
});

// Initialize panels from storage after DOM is ready
// (deduped: we are already inside the top-level DOMContentLoaded handler)
Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.prediction-card'), function(card) {
  var id    = card.getAttribute('data-set-id') || '';
  var panel = card.querySelector('.settings-panel');
  var toggle= card.querySelector('.settings-toggle');
  if (!panel || !toggle) return;

  var openKey = 'settingsOpen_' + id;
  // Default: panels start CLOSED on every load
  var isOpen = false;

  panel.classList.toggle('open', isOpen);
  panel.setAttribute('aria-hidden', isOpen ? 'false' : 'true');
  toggle.textContent = isOpen ? '\u2699\ufe0f Hide Settings' : '\u2699\ufe0f Show Settings';
  toggle.setAttribute('title', isOpen ? 'Hide Settings' : 'Show Settings');
  toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');
});

 
//  -  Compare All button functionality (robust change firing)  - 
var compareAllBtn = document.getElementById('compare-all-btn');

function fireFormEvents(el) {
  // Fire both 'input' and 'change' with bubbling to ensure listeners run
  ['input', 'change'].forEach(function(type) {
    el.dispatchEvent(new Event(type, { bubbles: true, cancelable: true }));
  });
}

if (compareAllBtn) {
  compareAllBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
    var boxes = document.querySelectorAll('.card-compare-checkbox');

    // 1) check them all first (sync)
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(boxes, function(cb){ cb.checked = true; });

    // 2) then, on the next frame, fire the events so the DOM state is settled
    requestAnimationFrame(function() {
      Array.prototype.forEach.call(boxes, function(cb) {
        ['input', 'change'].forEach(function(type) {
          cb.dispatchEvent(new Event(type, { bubbles: true, cancelable: true }));
        });
      });

      // 3) safety nudge per group to ensure its local update() runs
      Array.prototype.forEach.call(
        document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group'),
        function(group) {
          var first = group.querySelector('.card-compare-checkbox');
          if (first) {
            ['input', 'change'].forEach(function(type) {
              first.dispatchEvent(new Event(type, { bubbles: true, cancelable: true }));
            });
          }
        }
      );
    });
  });
}

// ============================================================
// SDI: Tab switcher + 3-dot dropdown  (ES5, no arrow fns)
// ============================================================
(function initSDI() {
  function activateTab(tabEl) {
    var bar   = tabEl.parentElement;
    var panel = tabEl.closest ? tabEl.closest('.lottery-collapsible-content') : null;
    if (!bar || !panel) return;
    var tabId = tabEl.getAttribute('data-sdi-tab');
    if (!tabId) return;
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(bar.querySelectorAll('.sdi-tab'), function(t) {
      var active = (t === tabEl);
      t.setAttribute('aria-selected', active ? 'true' : 'false');
      t.tabIndex = active ? 0 : -1;
    });
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(panel.querySelectorAll('.sdi-panel'), function(p) {
      p.style.display = (p.getAttribute('data-sdi-panel') === tabId) ? '' : 'none';
    });
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
    var t = ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('.sdi-tab') : null;
    if (t) activateTab(t);
  });
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(ev) {
    if (ev.key !== 'ArrowLeft' && ev.key !== 'ArrowRight') return;
    var t = ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('.sdi-tab') : null;
    if (!t) return;
    var all = Array.prototype.slice.call(t.parentElement.querySelectorAll('.sdi-tab'));
    var idx = all.indexOf(t);
    var next = ev.key === 'ArrowRight' ? all[(idx+1)%all.length] : all[(idx-1+all.length)%all.length];
    if (next) { next.focus(); activateTab(next); }
    ev.preventDefault();
  });
  // Initialize tab visibility on page load for every lottery group
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.sdi-tab-bar'), function(bar) {
    var active = bar.querySelector('.sdi-tab[aria-selected="true"]') ||
                 bar.querySelector('.sdi-tab');
    if (active) activateTab(active);
  });
}());

// Overview tab-chip navigation: clicking [data-skai-goto-tab] activates the named tab
// within the nearest lottery collapsible content ancestor.
// targetTabId is validated against a known allowlist before use in selector.
document.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
  var chip = ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('[data-skai-goto-tab]') : null;
  if (!chip) return;
  var targetTabId = chip.getAttribute('data-skai-goto-tab') || '';
  // Allowlist: only known tab IDs are accepted (prevents selector injection)
  var allowedTabs = { overview: 1, performance: 1, methods: 1, settings: 1 };
  if (!allowedTabs[targetTabId]) return;
  var content = chip.closest ? chip.closest('.lottery-collapsible-content') : null;
  if (!content) return;
  var targetTab = content.querySelector('.sdi-tab[data-sdi-tab="' + targetTabId + '"]');
  if (targetTab) {
    var bar = targetTab.parentElement;
    if (!bar) return;
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(bar.querySelectorAll('.sdi-tab'), function(t) {
      var active = (t === targetTab);
      t.setAttribute('aria-selected', active ? 'true' : 'false');
      t.tabIndex = active ? 0 : -1;
    });
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(content.querySelectorAll('.sdi-panel'), function(p) {
      p.style.display = (p.getAttribute('data-sdi-panel') === targetTabId) ? '' : 'none';
    });
    targetTab.focus();
  }
});

// Convert all timestamps to user's local timezone
// This runs after the DOM is loaded to convert ISO timestamps to local time
function convertTimestampsToLocal() {
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.local-time'), function(el) {
    var container = el.closest('[data-timestamp]');
    if (!container) return;
    
    var isoTime = container.getAttribute('data-timestamp');
    if (!isoTime) return;
    
    try {
      var date = new Date(isoTime);
      if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return;
      
      // Format: "Dec 30, 2025, 3:45pm"
      var options = {
        month: 'short',
        day: 'numeric',
        year: 'numeric',
        hour: 'numeric',
        minute: '2-digit',
        hour12: true
      };
      
      var localTime = date.toLocaleString('en-US', options);
      el.textContent = localTime;
    } catch (e) {
      // If conversion fails, leave the original timestamp
      console.error('Failed to convert timestamp:', isoTime, e);
    }
  });
}

// Run timestamp conversion after DOM is ready
convertTimestampsToLocal();

// Lottery section collapse/expand: restore initial state from localStorage.
// Click handling is done by data-lottery-toggle-btn="1" on the button.
function initLotteryCollapse() {
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group'), function(group) {
    var toggle = group.querySelector('.lottery-collapse-toggle');
    if (!toggle) return;

    var lotteryId = group.getAttribute('data-lottery-id');
    var baseLid    = lotteryId ? lotteryId.split('-')[0] : '';
    if (!lotteryId) return;

    // Restore collapsed state from localStorage
    try {
      if (localStorage.getItem('lottery_collapsed_' + (baseLid || lotteryId)) === 'true') {
        group.classList.add('collapsed');
        toggle.textContent = '\u25b6 Expand';
        toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
        toggle.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Expand lottery section');
      }
    } catch (e) {}
  });
}

// Initialize lottery collapse functionality
initLotteryCollapse();

// Set the initial label of the "Collapse All / Expand All" global button.
(function() {
  var allBtn = document.getElementById('mle-lottery-toggle-all-btn');
  if (!allBtn) { return; }
  var groups = document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group');
  var anyExpanded = false;
  for (var i = 0; i < groups.length; i++) {
    if (!groups[i].classList.contains('collapsed')) { anyExpanded = true; break; }
  }
  allBtn.textContent = anyExpanded ? '\u25bc Collapse All' : '\u25b6 Expand All';
}());

// Restore Prediction Results section collapse state from localStorage.
(function() {
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.prc-section'), function(sec) {
    var sectionId = sec.id;
    if (!sectionId) { return; }
    try {
      if (localStorage.getItem('prc_collapsed_' + sectionId) === 'true') {
        skaiPrcSetCollapsed(sec, true);
      }
    } catch (e) { /* localStorage unavailable (private browsing / quota) */ }
  });
})();

// ============================================================
// Strategy Workspace -- Overview tab, PRE-DRAW mode (ES5, no deps)
// ============================================================
(function() {
  'use strict';

  function esc(s) {
    // FIX: all replacements use valid quoted strings (no stray apostrophes)
    // ES5-safe; outputs HTML entities; UTF-8-safe.
    return String(s || '')
      .replace(/&/g, '\u0026amp;')
      .replace(/\u003c/g, '\u0026lt;')
      .replace(/\u003e/g, '\u0026gt;')
      .replace(/\u0022/g, '\u0026quot;')
      .replace(/\u0027/g, '\u0026#39;');
  }
  function initWorkspace(ws) {
    var lid      = ws.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
    var hasExtra = ws.getAttribute('data-sw-has-extra') === '1';
    var mainMax  = parseInt(ws.getAttribute('data-sw-main-max')  || '99', 10) || 99;
    var extraMax = parseInt(ws.getAttribute('data-sw-extra-max') || '9',  10) || 9;
    var predsRaw   = ws.getAttribute('data-sw-preds')   || '[]';
    var modulesRaw = ws.getAttribute('data-sw-modules') || '[]';
    var allPreds, modList;
    try { allPreds = JSON.parse(predsRaw); }   catch(e) { allPreds = []; console.warn('[SW] preds parse error:', e); }
    try { modList  = JSON.parse(modulesRaw); } catch(e) { modList  = []; console.warn('[SW] modules parse error:', e); }
    var srcTag = {skip_hit:'SK',ai_prediction:'NN',mcmc_prediction:'MC',heatmap:'FM',skai_prediction:'SKAI'};
    var activeSources = {}, builderMains = [], builderExtras = [], consensusSet = {};
    var toggles      = ws.querySelectorAll('.sw-source-toggle');
    var candidatesEl = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-candidates]');
    var poolEl       = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-pool]');
    var counterEl    = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-counter]');
    var countMains   = counterEl ? counterEl.querySelector('[data-sw-count-mains]')  : null;
    var countExtras  = counterEl ? counterEl.querySelector('[data-sw-count-extras]') : null;
    var addInput     = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-add-input]');
    var addBtn       = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-add-btn]');
    var rmWeakBtn    = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-remove-weak]');
    var clearBtn     = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-clear]');
    var saveSection  = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-save-section]');
    var saveMainsEl  = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-save-mains]');
    var saveExtrasEl = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-save-extras]');
    var saveSrcsEl   = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-save-sources]');
    var confLabel    = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-conf-label]');
    var confDetail   = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-conf-detail]');
    var confDots     = ws.querySelectorAll('[data-sw-dot]');
    var covList      = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-coverage-list]');
    var covTip       = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-cov-tip]');
    var balLabel     = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-bal-label]');
    var balDetail    = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-bal-detail]');
    var whlLabel     = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-wheel-label]');
    var whlDetail    = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-wheel-detail]');

    Array.prototype.forEach.call(toggles, function(cb) {
      activeSources[cb.getAttribute('data-sw-source')] = !!cb.checked;
    });

    function computeCandidates() {
      var bySource = {};
      allPreds.forEach(function(p) {
        if (!activeSources[p.source]) return;
        if (!bySource[p.source]) bySource[p.source] = {mains:[],extras:[]};
        p.mains.forEach(function(n) { if (bySource[p.source].mains.indexOf(n)===-1) bySource[p.source].mains.push(n); });
        p.extras.forEach(function(n){ if (bySource[p.source].extras.indexOf(n)===-1) bySource[p.source].extras.push(n); });
      });
      var sources = Object.keys(bySource), mainCount = {}, mainSrcs = {};
      sources.forEach(function(src) {
        bySource[src].mains.forEach(function(n) {
          mainCount[n] = (mainCount[n]||0)+1;
          mainSrcs[n]  = mainSrcs[n]||[];
          mainSrcs[n].push(srcTag[src]||src.substring(0,2).toUpperCase());
        });
      });
      consensusSet = {};
      Object.keys(mainCount).forEach(function(n){ if (mainCount[n]>=2) consensusSet[parseInt(n,10)]=true; });
      var all = Object.keys(mainCount).map(Number).sort(function(a,b){
        return mainCount[b]!==mainCount[a] ? mainCount[b]-mainCount[a] : a-b;
      });
      return {consensusNums:all.filter(function(n){return mainCount[n]>=2;}),
              supportingNums:all.filter(function(n){return 2 > mainCount[n];}),
              mainCount:mainCount, mainSrcs:mainSrcs, sources:sources};
    }

    function chipHtml(n,count,srcs){
      var c=count>=2, cls='sw-chip'+(c?' sw-chip--consensus':'');
      var bdg=c?'\u003cspan class="sw-chip-badge"\u003e'+count+'+\u003c/span\u003e':'';
      var tgs=srcs&&srcs.length?'\u003cspan class="sw-chip-srcs"\u003e['+srcs.join('][')+']\u003c/span\u003e':'';
      return '\u003cbutton class="'+cls+'" type="button" data-sw-chip-num="'+n+'"'+
             ' aria-label="Add '+n+' to strategy builder"\u003e'+esc(String(n))+bdg+tgs+'\u003c/button\u003e';
    }

    function renderCandidates(d) {
      if (!candidatesEl) return;
      if (!d.sources.length){candidatesEl.innerHTML='\u003cdiv class="sw-empty-state"\u003eSelect a source above.\u003c/div\u003e';return;}
      var h='';
      if (d.consensusNums.length){
        h+='\u003cdiv class="sw-candidate-group-label"\u003eConsensus ('+d.consensusNums.length+')\u003c/div\u003e\u003cdiv class="sw-chips"\u003e';
        d.consensusNums.forEach(function(n){h+=chipHtml(n,d.mainCount[n],d.mainSrcs[n]);});
        h+='\u003c/div\u003e';
      }
      if (d.supportingNums.length){
        h+='\u003cdiv class="sw-candidate-group-label" style="margin-top:.5rem;"\u003eSupporting ('+d.supportingNums.length+')\u003c/div\u003e\u003cdiv class="sw-chips"\u003e';
        d.supportingNums.forEach(function(n){h+=chipHtml(n,d.mainCount[n],d.mainSrcs[n]);});
        h+='\u003c/div\u003e';
      }
      candidatesEl.innerHTML=h||'\u003cdiv class="sw-empty-state"\u003eNo prediction numbers found.\u003c/div\u003e';
    }

    function renderPool(){
      if (!poolEl) return;
      if (!builderMains.length&&!builderExtras.length){
        poolEl.innerHTML='\u003cdiv class="sw-pool-empty"\u003eClick a candidate above to add numbers here.\u003c/div\u003e';
        if (saveSection) saveSection.style.display='none'; return;
      }
      var h='';
      builderMains.forEach(function(n){
        h+='\u003cbutton class="sw-pool-chip" type="button" data-sw-pool-num="'+n+'" data-sw-pool-type="main" aria-label="Remove '+n+'"\u003e'+esc(String(n))+'\u003cspan class="sw-pool-chip-x"\u003e\u00d7\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/button\u003e';
      });
      builderExtras.forEach(function(n){
        h+='\u003cbutton class="sw-pool-chip" style="background:#7c3aed;" type="button" data-sw-pool-num="'+n+'" data-sw-pool-type="extra" aria-label="Remove extra '+n+'"\u003e'+esc(String(n))+'(e)\u003cspan class="sw-pool-chip-x"\u003e\u00d7\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/button\u003e';
      });
      poolEl.innerHTML=h;
      if (saveSection) saveSection.style.display='';
    }

    function updateCounters(){
      if (countMains)  countMains.textContent=String(builderMains.length);
      if (countExtras) countExtras.textContent=String(builderExtras.length);
    }

    function updateSaveFields(){
      var ks=Object.keys(activeSources).filter(function(k){return activeSources[k];});
      if (saveMainsEl)  saveMainsEl.value=builderMains.join(',');
      if (saveExtrasEl) saveExtrasEl.value=builderExtras.join(',');
      if (saveSrcsEl)   saveSrcsEl.value=ks.join(',');
    }

    function updateIntelligence(){
      var tot=builderMains.length, con=builderMains.filter(function(n){return!!consensusSet[n];}).length;
      var rat=tot>0?con/tot:0;
      // Confidence
      var d=0,cs='\u2014',cc='';
      if(tot>0){if(rat>=0.8){cs='Strong';cc='sw-pos';d=5;}else if(rat>=0.5){cs='Moderate';cc='sw-pos';d=3;}else{cs='Low';cc='sw-caut';d=1;}}
      if(confLabel){confLabel.textContent=cs;confLabel.className='sw-intel-label '+cc;}
      if(confDetail)confDetail.textContent=tot>0?'Consensus: '+con+' of '+tot+' ('+Math.round(rat*100)+'%).':'Add numbers to see agreement strength.';
      Array.prototype.forEach.call(confDots,function(dot){
        var i=parseInt(dot.getAttribute('data-sw-dot')||'0',10),on=d >= i;
        dot.classList.toggle('active',on);dot.classList.toggle('high',on&&d>=4);
        dot.classList.toggle('caution',on&&d>0&&2>=d); // 2>=d avoids [..] Joomla filter match
      });
      // Coverage
      if(covList){
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(covList.querySelectorAll('.sw-coverage-item'),function(li){
          var m=li.getAttribute('data-sw-cov-method')||'',cv=false;
          if(tot>0)allPreds.forEach(function(p){if(p.source!==m)return;p.mains.forEach(function(n){if(builderMains.indexOf(n)!==-1)cv=true;});});
          li.classList.toggle('covered',cv);
          var chk=li.querySelector('.sw-coverage-check');if(chk)chk.innerHTML=cv?'\u2713':'\u2717';
        });
        var cc2=covList.querySelectorAll('.sw-coverage-item.covered').length;
        if(covTip)covTip.style.display=(tot>0&&2 > cc2)?'':'none';
      }
      // Balance
      if(tot===0){
        if(balLabel){balLabel.textContent='\u2014';balLabel.className='sw-intel-label';}
        if(balDetail)balDetail.textContent='Add numbers to check balance.';
      }else{
        var ht=false,hm=false;
        builderMains.forEach(function(n){allPreds.forEach(function(p){
          var ri=p.mains.indexOf(n);if(ri===-1)return;var rk=ri+1;
          if(3>=rk)ht=true;if(rk>=4&&10>=rk)hm=true; // >=forms avoid [..] Joomla filter match
        });});
        var bs,bc;
        if(ht&&hm){bs='Balanced';bc='sw-pos';}else if(ht){bs='Top-heavy';bc='sw-caut';}else if(hm){bs='Mid-heavy';bc='sw-caut';}else{bs='Unknown';bc='';}
        if(balLabel){balLabel.textContent=bs;balLabel.className='sw-intel-label '+bc;}
        if(balDetail)balDetail.textContent=(ht&&hm)?'Good mix of top and mid-rank numbers.':(ht?'Mostly top-rank. Try adding mid-rank numbers (#4\u201310).':'Mostly mid-rank. Try adding a top-rank number (#1\u20133).');
      }
      // Wheel Readiness
      var ws2,wc,wn;
      if(tot===0){ws2='\u2014';wc='';wn='Add at least 10 main numbers.';}
      else if(tot>=15){ws2='Wheel-ready: Yes';wc='sw-pos';wn=tot===15?'15 numbers is a common wheel base.':'Large enough for most wheeling systems.';}
      else if(tot>=10){ws2='Wheel-ready: Maybe';wc='sw-caut';wn='Small set ('+tot+' mains). Add more for a larger wheel.';}
      else{ws2='Wheel-ready: No';wc='sw-warn';wn='Need at least 10 main numbers ('+tot+' so far).';}
      if(whlLabel){whlLabel.textContent=ws2;whlLabel.className='sw-intel-label '+wc;}
      if(whlDetail)whlDetail.textContent=wn;
    }

    function refresh(){
      var d=computeCandidates();
      renderCandidates(d);renderPool();updateCounters();updateSaveFields();updateIntelligence();
    }

    function addTo(n,isE){
      n=parseInt(n,10);if(!(typeof (n) === 'number' && isFinite(n))||1 > n)return;
      if(isE){if(n>extraMax)return;if(builderExtras.indexOf(n)===-1)builderExtras.push(n);builderExtras.sort(function(a,b){return a-b;});}
      else{if(n>mainMax)return;if(builderMains.indexOf(n)===-1)builderMains.push(n);builderMains.sort(function(a,b){return a-b;});}
      refresh();
    }
    function rmFrom(n,isE){
      n=parseInt(n,10);
      if(isE)builderExtras=builderExtras.filter(function(x){return x!==n;});
      else   builderMains=builderMains.filter(function(x){return x!==n;});
      refresh();
    }

    Array.prototype.forEach.call(toggles,function(cb){
      cb.addEventListener('change',function(){activeSources[cb.getAttribute('data-sw-source')]=!!cb.checked;refresh();});
    });
    if(candidatesEl)candidatesEl.addEventListener('click',function(ev){
      var b=ev.target.closest?ev.target.closest('[data-sw-chip-num]'):null;
      if(b)addTo(b.getAttribute('data-sw-chip-num'),false);
    });
    if(poolEl)poolEl.addEventListener('click',function(ev){
      var b=ev.target.closest?ev.target.closest('[data-sw-pool-num]'):null;
      if(!b)return;rmFrom(b.getAttribute('data-sw-pool-num'),b.getAttribute('data-sw-pool-type')==='extra');
    });
    if(addBtn&&addInput){
      addBtn.addEventListener('click',function(){addTo(addInput.value,false);addInput.value='';addInput.focus();});
      addInput.addEventListener('keydown',function(ev){if(ev.key==='Enter'){ev.preventDefault();addTo(addInput.value,false);addInput.value='';}});
    }
    if(rmWeakBtn)rmWeakBtn.addEventListener('click',function(){builderMains=builderMains.filter(function(n){return!!consensusSet[n];});refresh();});
    if(clearBtn)clearBtn.addEventListener('click',function(){builderMains=[];builderExtras=[];refresh();});
    refresh();
  }

  function bootSW(){
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('[data-sw-workspace]'),initWorkspace);
  }
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',bootSW);}
  else{bootSW();}
}());
// close the top-level DOMContentLoaded wrapper opened at the start of this script
});

/* ===== merged script section ===== */

  function scrollToFavorites() {
    var el = document.getElementById('favorite-lotteries');
    if (!el) {
      return;
    }

    // Respect users who prefer reduced motion
    var prefersReduced =
      window.matchMedia &&
      window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches;

    if (prefersReduced) {
      // Jump without animation
      el.scrollIntoView(true);
    } else if (el.scrollIntoView) {
      try {
        el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
      } catch (e) {
        // Fallback for older browsers
        el.scrollIntoView(true);
      }
    }

    // Make the region programmatically focusable and move focus for screen readers
    if (!el.hasAttribute('tabindex')) {
      el.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
    }
    try {
      el.focus();
    } catch (e) {}

    el.classList.add('highlighted-scroll');
    setTimeout(function () {
      el.classList.remove('highlighted-scroll');
    }, 2000);
  }

/* ===== merged script section ===== */

// ============================================================
// Best Settings Snapshot: jump handlers
// "View best" scrolls to a prediction card; "All runs" scrolls
// to the lottery group. ES5-compatible.
// ============================================================
(function initSnapshotJumps() {
  var snap = document.getElementById('skai-global-snapshot');
  if (!snap) { return; }

  snap.addEventListener('click', function (ev) {
    var btn = ev.target;
    if (!btn || btn.tagName !== 'BUTTON') { return; }

    // Helper: smooth scroll with fallback for older browsers
    function scrollTo(el) {
      if (!el) { return; }
      try {
        el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
      } catch (e) {
        el.scrollIntoView(true);
      }
    }

    // "View best"  -  jump to the prediction card for this run
    if (btn.classList.contains('skai-bss-view-btn')) {
      var runId = btn.getAttribute('data-jump-run-id') || '';
      var lid   = btn.getAttribute('data-jump-lottery-id') || '';
      if (runId) {
        // Look for the card by data-set-id first
        var card = document.querySelector('[data-set-id="' + runId + '"]');
        if (card) {
          scrollTo(card);
          return;
        }
      }
      // Fallback: scroll to the lottery group
      if (lid) {
        var grps = document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group');
        for (var i = 0; i < grps.length; i++) {
          var grpLid = (grps[i].getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '').split('-')[0];
          if (grpLid === String(lid)) {
            scrollTo(grps[i]);
            return;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // "All runs"  -  jump to the lottery group for this lottery
    if (btn.classList.contains('skai-bss-all-link')) {
      var crrId = btn.getAttribute('data-jump-crr-id') || '';
      if (crrId) {
        var grps2 = document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group');
        for (var j = 0; j < grps2.length; j++) {
          var grpLid2 = (grps2[j].getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '').split('-')[0];
          if (grpLid2 === String(crrId)) {
            scrollTo(grps2[j]);
            return;
          }
        }
      }
    }
  });
})();

/* ===== merged script section ===== */

// ============================================================
// DEBUG: Prediction Results section diagnostics.
// Set to true to log draw-lookup details to the console.
// ES5-compatible; safe to leave in production (false = silent).
// ============================================================
var DEBUG_PRED_RESULTS = false;
// Override via URL query string: append ?debug_pred_results=1 to enable without redeployment
if (window.location.search && window.location.search.indexOf('debug_pred_results=1') !== -1) {
  DEBUG_PRED_RESULTS = true;
}

(function () {
  if (!DEBUG_PRED_RESULTS) { return; }
  var sections = document.querySelectorAll('.prc-section');
  for (var i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
    var sec = sections[i];
    var pending = sec.querySelectorAll('.prc-row-pending');

    console.log('[PRED-RESULTS] section:', sec.id,
      '| total rows:', total.length,
      '| upcoming rows:', pending.length);
    var upcomingRows = sec.querySelectorAll('tr.prc-row-pending');
    for (var j = 0; j < upcomingRows.length; j++) {
      var cells = upcomingRows[j].querySelectorAll('td');
      console.log('  [UPCOMING] draw date:', cells[1] ? cells[1].textContent.trim() : '?',
        'method:', cells[2] ? cells[2].textContent.trim() : '?');
    }
  }
